Foreign Rice Currently, it is the end of the year, and the market has been quiet. Yesterday, because inland merchants actively bought broken foreign rice, this street was also tempted. In addition to the existing broken rice, they also competed to buy "road goods" (路貨, goods in transit) and recently arrived broken rice. A total of 400 bags of existing broken rice were transacted, along with 750 bags of "road goods" arriving in three to four days, 100 tons for January delivery, and 1,000 tons for February delivery. Selling prices were all raised by several fen. Digestion of Saigon machine-milled rice remained weak, with only 300 bags of existing goods and 400 tons of futures transacted. The market closed steady.

客秈 (Ke Xian) In recent days, arrivals have been low. Previously, "ke hua" (客化, merchant digestion) was not strong, and the market was stagnant. Yesterday, in addition to continued purchases by this street, inland digestion was also very active. Furthermore, Chongsha merchants competed for purchases. However, existing stocks in the market were scarce, and merchants planned to hold onto their goods until the next lunar new year before selling. Due to the eager buying of the "ke bang," prices immediately rose by over one jiao.

Only Yellow Soybeans Are Being Transacted Among Miscellaneous Grains 200

In yesterday's miscellaneous grains market, only the local merchants were actually buying. Those not in immediate need were concluding their business. The total market saw over 500 bags of Hankou Zha soybeans transacted, priced at 3.82 to 3.69 yuan. There were also 100 bags of Hankou late soybeans transacted, priced at 3.6 yuan, and 300 bags of Shashi soybeans, priced at 3.69 to 3.65 yuan.

Sugar Market: Guangdong Coarse Granulated White Sugar Falls Again by Three Jiao 201

The sugar market trend remained weak yesterday. The association's price setting included the Sugar Industry Cooperative selling 10,000 bags of 24 coarse granulated white sugar for March-April delivery at a price of 2.675 Dutch guilders, up 1.5 fen from the previous increase. Furthermore, the original quantity of Guangdong coarse granulated white sugar was 1,360 bags, with a bid price of 18 yuan, down another 3 jiao. Only 50 bags of spot goods were transacted, and 300 bags of re-exported goods were transacted at 4.5 jiao above the spot price. The local factory's refined white sugar remained unchanged. Brokers offered Zhuang Qing at 10.34 yuan, Huanggang Qing at 10.1 yuan, 10 yuan, and Longgang Qing at 9.8 jiao, and lower grades at 6 jiao, for over 1,000 bags transacted. Because these goods would not be available until next Wednesday or Thursday, the offered price was relatively low.

Northern and Southern Goods: Raw Peanuts Gradually Rise by Three to Four Jiao 202

Raw peanuts are trending steadily higher in Qingdao in recent days, and quoted prices here are extremely firm. Previously, prices rose by three to four jiao. High-quality Kaifeng peanuts once reached 8.1 yuan. Yesterday, merchants from Guangdong and Shantou imported another 500 tons. The quality of Kaifeng peanuts was relatively lower, priced at 8 yuan, Lanfeng peanuts at 7.7 jiao, and Xuzhou peanuts at 6.5 yuan.

Silk and Tea: Moroccan Green Tea Sales Remain Good 203

French Morocco is a very large market for our country's green tea consumption. Last year, the amount of Chinese tea imported into that port totaled more than 320,000 boxes, which is very significant. According to news from that area, green teas such as Zhenmei, Lamei, Zhenmei, and Xiumei from Shangzhong Zhuang in our country, such as goods from Tunxi, Wuyuan, and Suian, have seen a sharp increase in sales due to the promotion of abstinence from alcohol by the Hui people on various islands. However, due to the poor harvest of agricultural products last year, the market is sluggish and tea prices have not risen. In addition, for the item of Tuzhuang Zhenmei, because some of the boxed tea shipped last year did not match the bottom (of the box), its reputation has been greatly diminished compared to the Zhuang goods from inland areas.

Metals: British Huisi Iron Supply Cannot Meet Demand 204

British Huisi iron of 112 pounds and 200 pounds are reporting low inventories, and new shipments are limited. Therefore, the circulation of goods in the market often cannot meet the demand. Due to environmental factors, the standard has gradually risen. The current price per box (calculated at 200 pounds) is estimated at 26.5 to 27 yuan, which is a good 5 jiao to 1 yuan higher than before. It is reported that sales to cigarette companies have been very strong in recent days.

East White Iron Import Price Falls by Four Fen 205

Yesterday's telegram indicated that the import price of East White Iron fell by another four fen. It is estimated that each 3-foot by 7-foot sheet is priced at 1 yuan and 1 jiao, and each 3-foot by 6-foot sheet is priced at 8.6 jiao. However, few traders in this port are purchasing.

Free Talk

On Types and Heroes 216

— Zhang Xiangshan

In literary works, when the protagonist lacks typicality, they often become imaginary characters, a kind of dreamlike bas-relief. In the works of naturalistic and realistic writers, the protagonist must conform to actual people, comprehensively creating a type of active figure in real society.

Regarding typicality, it is not an abstract reproduction of the protagonist's character, but a concrete, living human being through the writer's progressive worldview. Often, many writers, loyal to everything in the present world, although able to meticulously describe similar, more typical characters, these characters are often trapped in an ordinary life, lacking courageous heroism.

In Chekhov's works, there are comprehensive protagonists of the melancholy era of Nicholas, doctors, or children. In Cervantes' Don Quixote, there is a humorous and exaggerated knight. In Turgenev's Rudin, there is the smooth-talking but always-obstructed Rudin. I believe these types indeed concretely represent the living humanity of that time, but in terms of their role in literary works, they are of little use. At the same time, in Shakespeare's four major tragedies, these typical protagonists concretely express the fate of the decline of the aristocratic class. Generally speaking, the former are all negative types, while the latter carry a positive nature. As for the protagonists in the works of romantic writers, they are not typical, but fantasies; to give the most obvious example, Dorian Gray in Oscar Wilde's "The Picture of Dorian Gray" is the best example.

In past literary works and in the works of various writers today, I believe that although the reality of the protagonist has been recognized, and realists are not seen as mere mirrors, and especially attention has been paid to typicality, yet in terms of shortcomings, they still commit the rules of schematic formulas, and are ordinary rather than heroic.

The waterline author Glatkov said in his report: "As a shortcoming in our works, in the guiding places, there is a lack of creative, moving, and appealing typical images of human beings." Fadeev also said, "In the writing of modern protagonists, many have not yet been liberated from schematicism, and lack typical characters in typical events."

Indeed, regarding the error of schematicism, I can recall Xiaolin Duoxieer's "Numaziri Village." This novel is less of a novel and more of an iron formula, turning the protagonist's character into a figure cast from a schematic mold. This kind of description and creation may create an atmosphere of heroism, but it is no longer a real, living human being. To obtain a truly human and typical character, one must start from a living life. Resolutions and books cannot impart true character, they can only provide a mold for creating that life, but this is not true art.

We must take the progressive figures of the present era as the object of research and reflection, and we must understand what they live by, how they rejoice, what they dream of, how they love, what they grieve, what they fight for, and how they work, and what kind of thinking patterns they hold, and so on! Infuse these images with extreme intensity, make them shine, and mold them into levers of the advanced thought of our era.

According to the above writing method, I believe that the character portrayed will definitely be typical, and also a hero of the times. The hero here is not a hero transcending the times, but a "common hero" forged by the power of the masses (this phrase may be problematic). To give a practical example, Guo Ruhe in "The Iron Flood," Tiefensheng in "The Rout," and Davidov in "Virgin Soil Upturned," etc., all belong to this type of hero. We know that these heroes are not superhuman figures in history, or figures who open up the world by their personal strength, but figures who exert their personal abilities by instilling the will of the masses. Let me record a section of Serafimovich's analysis of Guo Ruhe:

"Guo Ruhe is a hero, and also not a hero, because if the masses do not make him their leader, if the masses do not inject him with ideas, then Guo Ruhe is a most ordinary person. But, at the same time, he is also a hero, because the masses not only inject him with ideas, but also follow him; obey him as they obey a leader."

Looking at this explanation, one can clearly understand the true face of the hero I am talking about. Such heroes not only increase the positive and real aspects of the work, but also do not lead to blind and ambiguous behavior. The type of Don Quixote, who boasts of being a hero and can fight windmills, will not be reproduced in today's literature. And the figure who is proven by a positive formula will probably no longer appear in his rigid posture!

Thief (Part 2) 217

— Cao Ming

One day, when the river was high, Ma Jiaju, a nineteen-year-old, cast his small net by the river. He puffed on a rolled cigarette, chatting with Aunt Lanxiang, a woman in her forties, who was washing clothes at the "dock." As usual, Ba Guan, the fourteen-year-old only son of the village chief, Master Ma, kept taking small stones out of his large pocket and patrolled the riverside. When he spotted a place to cast a net, he would throw the stones down. Because of this, Ma Jiaju and his companions often made threatening gestures at him, pretending to fight.

"It's not a joke if you hit my head. You don't even know how to swim, in front of the Dragon King of the Sea... Be careful, I'll tell your dad," Aunt Lanxiang, who was squatting on the stone steps by the water, looked up and warned.

"I'm practicing my eyesight; I'll switch to bullets later. ...It's okay if you die, when I become a big official, I'll build you a memorial arch," Ba Guan giggled and threw another stone at the woman.

Ma Jiaju suddenly spread his arms fiercely, picked up a blue brick, and chased after the thin little monkey. As if fate had set a trap, intentionally plunging the young fisherman into eternal misery, Ba Guan ran as if flying, running very far, and suddenly fell into the water...

Ma Jiaju cried out in shock, not knowing what to do. Later, when he made up his mind to jump into the water to save him, it was already too late. He bore a terrible charge and was sentenced to seven years in prison. And Aunt Lanxiang, because she told the truth to prove his innocence, got a purple fingerprint on her face, and had to pay for her own eye treatment.

Afterwards, the first time he appeared in the village was when he was surrounded and beaten by the waiters in front of a restaurant. After that, he was always cursed, beaten, and driven away by the whole village. There was no trace of the kind fisherman.

"In the past, people used power to crush you. Now, how are you going to answer them? Alas, I pity you, I pity your mother. If there is still justice in the world..." She looked up, a hopeful light in her eyes, looking at the thin, tall young man in front of her. "Counting, you're only twenty-eight years old, yes, a twenty-eight-year-old, at least there's still half of you left... On the day of the Tai Sui Festival, I'll make you a pair of shoes, so you can walk on the right path properly. Twenty-eight years old, um, it's not too late..."

The man stood up without any emotion, smiling slyly. "I'm going my right path now. I haven't had lunch yet, that cigarette lighter box can probably be exchanged for forty cents." He strode away, swaying.

The old woman squinted her eyes, staring at his back, and muttered to herself: "Poor, a fellow hated by everyone..." She hunched over and ran into the house, preparing to fetch firewood hoops to bundle up the scattered firewood.

When she came out, moving her small feet, which had been destroyed and recorded the ugly deeds of mankind, she found that her blue grain water pipe and her firewood axe were gone. She was stunned for a moment, then angrily, yet sluggishly, stomped her small feet. "A fiend who has lost all conscience, using your skills on an old widow." She shouted loudly, shielding her eyes from the sun, and looked around the streets and alleys. After a while, she called out to the empty alley in a more affectionate tone:

"Ma Zai, you conscienceless thing, you...you must come and get your shoes, on the day of the Tai Sui Festival, come to me to get your shoes!" (End)

Waiting 218

— Zu

Morning. The season is early winter.

Outside the window is black. A pair of sleepless eyes look at the black, but for a long, long time, it is still black outside the window. I remember there are two lilac trees outside the window, a hemp rope hanging from the window, and a broken bowl for feeding the dog; but now the lilac trees are black, the hemp rope is black, and the broken bowl is also black.

Facing the window is the door, I also remember that the door is dark purple, but now the door is also black.

When will it be dawn?

The sleepless eyes are hungry, longing for sleep. If they sleep, they will wake up and see the sun, but this is naturally a luxury. Then, give up sleep and wait for the sun, but while waiting, it is still black outside the window.

It seems like it will always be like this, without rotation, without change, without different colors, without different sounds, like a stagnant pool, like a long rain, like a hot summer, like a hard journey. You have to be patient and endure this suffering. You hope that one day in a deathly silent pool, there will suddenly be ripples and the movement of aquatic plants; but in front of your eyes, it is clearly a stagnant pool, dead silence, dead decay!

That's right, you can't get rid of your impatience with the tedious and long rain. You hope that someday, will a bit of sunlight pierce through the millions of layers of dust-covered clouds. You think of the beauty of the blue sky, and the greenness of life under the blue sky; but in front of your eyes, it is clearly a patch of gloom, from dawn to dusk, there is always rain hanging in front of the eaves, and it seems that your heart is always wet.

I say this is like a hot summer, can you endure the oppressive heat? Recall the sweltering heat of Jiangnan this year. At that time, you could only beg the sky to bestow a thunderstorm, a breeze, or a cloudy day tomorrow. But the sky did not move a bit, as if it would always be so unfeeling. Your heart is burning with fire, and your soul is about to melt into a liquid!

I am also not overly using a difficult journey as a metaphor, because I have tasted the suffering of the steerage of a sea ship. In this place, you need a solid body and a tolerant personality to resist filth, suffering, and humiliation. There, you do not believe that time is moving. The ship says that it will arrive at its destination the day after tomorrow, and you doubt when is the day after tomorrow. Outside the round window, the size of a plate, it is always the sea, the sea, a sea so blue it is about to turn black.

The world is stagnant, with only one color, one sound. Before my eyes are stagnant water, long rain, hot summer, and a hard journey! I look at the black, black, black!

Didn't I say that the black door is facing the black window? Suddenly, the black door turned, and a child and the lights of the corridor outside the door appeared at the broken gap of the black door. The child put a bottle of milk on the table (my roommate is an undernourished young man) and gently closed the door.

After a while, I saw a faint glimmer of dawn outside the black window, but I doubted whether it was dawn yet?

Dusk at Tongguan 219

— Yan Jikuan

Three years ago.

On that sweltering summer day, as the sun kissed the treetops, my friend Mian'an and I arrived at the strategically important Tongguan Pass. The city wall perched diagonally on the hillside, its imposing presence striking. To the east, a motor road led to Hangu Pass; to the west, a motor road led to Xi'an. The Wei River flowed into the Yellow River here. Without a doubt, it was the key fortress of Shaanxi, and the gateway to Shaanxi.

We got out of the car for a short rest, then agreed to visit the city wall. The hillside was very steep, and the wall followed it upwards; we had to climb step by step, because the mountain and the wall were both steep. Halfway up, we looked around. Outside was a deep valley, and inside was a steep downward slope. One careless step would surely lead to being smashed to pieces. At this point, half the sun had already sunk below the horizon, and weak rays of light shone through the thin clouds, which made us even more fearful. However, we couldn't satisfy our curiosity without reaching the summit, so we summoned our courage and continued to climb. Indeed, my heart was filled with fear, a fear that made it beat erratically. Neither of us wanted to show weakness, so we silently pushed forward, finally reaching the peak of the mountain. Looking around, to the south were towering, overlapping mountain peaks, seemingly submerged in hazy clouds; to the north was the Yellow River, like a white ribbon, flowing from the distant, indistinct horizon to the distant, indistinct horizon. Standing before this majestic mountain pass and the torrential river, one couldn't help but feel how insignificant one was.

Time passed imperceptibly. A vast twilight enveloped us. We couldn't leisurely gaze at the mountains and rivers before us, or reminisce about past events in our hearts. We had to rouse our spirits and carefully descend step by step. Our motto was to move forward, not to look left or right, and we would safely reach our destination. As expected, as the night curtain fully opened, we returned to the quaint inn.

Dinghu and Feishui Pool 220

— Li Sanlang

Dinghu Lake, shrouded in a deathly silence, appears from afar as a tall peak standing in the clouds. At the foot of the mountain, one can hear the refreshing sea breeze rustling through the treetops, its uniquely beautiful melodies playing perpetually. When walking along the winding mountain path with its nine curves and thirteen bends, one can hear the always-pessimistic and mournful bells of the Buddhist temple, giving travelers the feeling that this is a secluded paradise. The lush green leaves block the spring sun, making travelers feel the coolness here. On the mountainside, with its ever-changing scenery, one can never get enough of the beautiful daytime views.

In Dinghu, one can see many historical sites. When Su Dongpo was exiled to Southern Yue, he often hid here and spent his days in solitude. Beside the natural beauty of Feishui Pool, in the pavilion, he wrote many poems filled with lament.

At Feishui Pool, which is over thirty feet high, a snow-white waterfall, four feet wide, pours down after tracing an arc. The rushing sound, like ten thousand horses galloping, reverberates across several valleys. The white water glistens under the warm sun. The deep, clear pool is a rare swimming spot in the hot summer.

However, as I silently leaned on the smooth stone slab, gazing at the sun in the sky, it stirred up endless thoughts.

This place is not the human world; perhaps it is merely a haven for weary misanthropes.

The Human World (10) 221

— Li Huiying

"Yan Yan, Mr. Jin is here."

Xiao Ju didn't answer Mr. Jin's question; instead, she shouted. The woman of the house hurriedly called from the west room:

"Please sit down in the east room and have some good tea."

Judging by this, he must be an important guest. We didn't receive such a welcoming and flattering reception. I thought I could see what kind of person this important guest, Mr. Jin, was.

"He's Korean."

As soon as this guest entered the room, I recognized his nationality. A Korean is just like a Japanese. No matter what clothes they wear, they can be recognized at once. However, I can't explain why. You can't say that Koreans and Japanese have certain features etched on their faces. Then I thought about his relationship with this family. He's probably the owner of this private opium den, a lackey of the Japanese. Xiao Ju brought him tea and cigarettes. His arrogant manner suggested that he didn't see any of the living things or inanimate objects in the room.

"This thing, he deserves a good whack on the head."

I was indignant and wanted to argue with him, dissatisfied with his pretense. Actually, we're all slaves of subjugated nations, so why hold onto such thoughts? But I was still angry with him.

"This is -"

So when Xiao Ju wanted to introduce us, I waved my hand to stop her. At this time, the woman of the house and my friend came in, one after another.

The woman of the house seemed to have forgotten about me, her customer. She didn't greet me but only exchanged polite words with the Korean, then asked him to give her another day of grace.

There must be a financial relationship between them.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Discussions

Bank Investments to Aid Rural Areas 222

— Xing An

In recent years, the Chinese countryside has been gradually collapsing, a hard truth. Therefore, the urgent need for rural relief has become a pressing task. Recently, cries of rural collapse have arisen everywhere across the country. Following these cries is the call for rural relief. However, relief is still relief, and collapse is still collapse. Can rural relief be achieved by merely shouting a few slogans? No matter how grand the rural relief plan may be, to reverse the misfortune of today's countryside, it is necessary to work step by step in a practical manner; empty talk is of no use.

Recently, I heard that the banking industry in this city is considering investing in rural relief. Because the banking industry in this city, recognizing the economic decline in the interior, has been investing in relief with considerable success in the past one or two years. Since last year, all industries in this city have been extremely depressed, leading to a concentration of huge sums of money in the banking sector, which in turn has made lending difficult. At the same time, although investing in rural areas may have thin profits and be labor-intensive, it is reliable in terms of credit. Therefore, the banks have decided to strive to engage in rural investment starting this year. If rural management develops, all industries will progress accordingly. And the banks themselves will also be consolidated. This is very good news.

In recent years, the economic situation of Chinese society has presented a distorted development. On the one hand, due to the impact of the world economic panic and the blows of natural and man-made disasters, not only has the rural economy of the whole country been scorched, but also the general industrial and commercial sectors have faced financial difficulties. On the other hand, the banking industry has been booming and showing a unique prosperity. For example, last year, all banks in this city had considerable surpluses, especially the Central Bank and the other three banks. However, the result of the development of the banking industry is the excess of idle capital and the concentration of idle capital in cities. This is not only not beneficial to the national economy, but also detrimental to the banking industry itself. If the excess of idle capital can be used for the construction of productive enterprises, the declining productive enterprises of our country may not be able to develop because of it. However, the banking industry itself, due to various reasons, cannot transfer this idle capital to productive enterprises, but instead uses it for speculative transactions (such as real estate and public debt investments). In this way, not only do industrial and commercial sectors not receive relief from the banks, but also the future of the banking industry is not very promising. Therefore, although the banking industry can maintain a good situation on the surface during this time of economic depression, it is actually still unsound.

As for the plan now, if the banking industry wants to fulfill its own duties, it should broaden its horizons and put all the huge amount of idle capital it has absorbed not only in warehouses or used for illegitimate purposes, but as much as possible in supporting the construction of productive enterprises. This will not only give the banking industry's idle capital a legitimate outlet and enable it to develop day by day, but also give all industries, including agriculture, industry, and commerce, the hope of restoring prosperity. The country and society will benefit greatly.

Reproductive Competition 223

— You Qi

People must get married when they reach a certain age; the reason for this lies in the need for "physiology." Even if limited by economic ability, it is not possible to hold the wedding as desired, the component of that "need" will not be reduced or weakened as a result. Isn't that so? In the big cities, news of "adultery" is constantly appearing? Isn't it constantly churning out new tricks?

However, some people, I don't know if they are deliberately playing dumb or intentionally blaming, have asked me this: "According to you, it seems that the highest expectation of marriage is 'physiology,' but young men in the countryside have not yet reached the time of 'need' in terms of 'physiology,' so why do they still have to get married?" This, it seems, is not worth raising, because the reason is too obvious.

Regardless of whether marriage is needed or not, the childbearing after marriage "is an inevitable natural phenomenon," although many people are suffering, crying, and even grieving under this phenomenon.

Really, having children after marriage increases the burden, and when the burden becomes too heavy, it can stifle the breath, and you can't turn over like falling into a bale of cotton. So the heart is regretting, not marrying so early, but what's the use of regretting?

Friends, practice abstinence and reduce our burden a little!

I had to let out such a sigh. However, people are, after all, animals with spirituality, the most sensitive animals with spirituality. When you feel regret, you will "hate" it, but when you stop being dominated by physiology and are in need, the previous hate will disappear without a trace. "Abstinence" and "birth control" will not exist, and maybe you will punish yourself afterward.

In order to cope with this established environment, it is shrouded in a layer of sad mist in the old ways. However, opening yesterday's newspaper, in Toronto, USA, Mrs. Panadu and Mrs. Ganey are working hard to produce for the sake of competing for Mr. Miller's "fertility bonus," and in order to show the speed of their production, Panadu boasts to Ganey that she has no chance of winning. Naturally, Ganey is also unwilling to remain silent, so she is "making persistent efforts." Really, counting from 1926, with a limit of ten years, then, there are only two years left until the deadline.

In the end, boasting is not the truth. Mrs. Ganey's rate exceeded Panadu's. She gave birth to eleven children in eight years, which cannot be said to be an amazing number.

But, what about when you check yourself again? Don't say "competition," even "preservation" seems not to be an easy thing!

Random Thoughts on a New Home 224

— Hua Mu

Having lived in the core of Shanghai - in a house in a lane - for a long time, I am used to hearing the noisy sounds of the city from morning to night, and the cries of food vendors who disturb people's sweet dreams every night, regardless of the cold winter or hot summer. As time went on, I gradually didn't find them so annoying or noisy. Dawn and midnight have become a familiar habit, cutting through quite a bit of loneliness. Now, I suddenly moved to this small town a few minutes by car from Shanghai. The first night, what I wasn't used to and what I felt was cold and lonely was that I couldn't hear the familiar melodies of these habitual sounds. Because of this situation, I regretted it, as if I had done something big that was displeasing to my heart, and I felt restless and infinitely lonely.

That was the bad impression I got of my new home on the first night. I barely got more than two hours of peaceful sleep all night. It was as if I had suddenly been placed alone in a desolate mountain temple. The solemn quietness of the deep mountains and valleys made me unable to bear it, giving rise to a feeling of terror, scratching at my nerves, and not allowing me a moment of peace.

Occasionally, there were a few barks from farmhouses in distant villages, and the low sound of a steam whistle that was almost inaudible. These intermittent and weak, sad sounds did not reduce the feeling of loneliness at night. Those few unfamiliar barks were even more terrifying, as if they were the mournful groans of a weak soul suffering, making one's hair stand on end and shivering. Several times I heard these terrible cries, I had to cover my head with a blanket.

Before twelve o'clock, I could also hear the sound of trains rumbling by a few times. It suddenly shook my nerves, and I felt a little comfort, increasing the activity of my blood flow. However, this was very short-lived. After the train gradually went away, the situation returned to its original state, and the situation was even worse. It was as if a firecracker had been set off in a deep valley, leaving behind only a clearer emptiness and calmness, making my nerves suddenly lose their support, hanging in the air and unable to grasp the edge, so empty and unbearable.

The first night was really hard to get through. I simply suffered a night of injustice. The suffering of insomnia during that year of illness made me shake my head in fear whenever I thought of it. Other suffering can be endured, or it is very possible that I can get used to it after a long time? The only thing I worry about is that I am afraid of getting insomnia because of this situation. That sin is enough for me to bear. However, whether I can escape this unknown difficulty in the future is quite a matter of conjecture.

Now let's talk about the situation on the second night. This is really a miracle - it is foreseeable that the discovery of this miracle may make my situation even worse. Can you guess what this miracle is? It turned out that it was about three o'clock in the second half of the night. As I was drowsy, suddenly, a sharp and extremely sad pig's cry pierced my ears. I couldn't help but be surprised, and my slightly peaceful nerves became restless again. The cries were initially high-pitched and sad, but after a while, there was suddenly a shrill, desperate cry, which was clearly the last struggle of that poor, stupid creature, and then there was silence. At this time, my nerves were so hard to bear that they were about to explode, and there was simply no way to calm down. Red blood, white knives, a struggling, trembling soul, the fierce, cruel, and disgusting face of a wolf - a tragic scene of a slaughterhouse was clearly presented before me. I tried my best to close my eyes, trying to avoid and stop this association. But the result of my efforts was even worse. What was struggling was no longer a pig but a person, and there was an extra bloody head, an open, pale mouth, dismembered limbs, and a steaming, bouncing, bright red heart... That's how I spent the night in a nightmare until dawn. The tragic cries also recurred intermittently until dawn.

However, things in the world are always to be manipulated by others, and there is no room for one's own will to control and choose. For this reason, although this new home has so many reasons why it is uninhabitable, there is nothing I can do about it, so I have to bite the bullet and live here.

Opening "Bewitching"

The Fan family in the ruined garden is in Pingyang. There are many fox spirits causing trouble. There is a Ning Sheng among them. He does not believe in demons and reads books. He came to the thorny place wrapped in a quilt. He is not greedy for wealth or lust. They all know that after eating, he lies by the window. There is a charming fox spirit appearing. You have not heard that Tu Shan helped the Xia God Wan. He guided the water to flow into the Huai River, and his merits were evident. You are reading books and misunderstanding the books. Living by the Stream by Liu Zongyuan

For a long time, I have been bound by officialdom. Fortunately, I was banished to this southern barbarian land. I idly rely on the farms next door. I occasionally seem like a mountain forest guest. I plow the dew-covered grass in the morning. I lean against the echoing stream at night. I come and go without meeting anyone. I sing a long song to the blue sky of Chu.

Border Song by Wang Changling

Watering horses crossing the autumn water, the water is cold and the wind is like a knife. The sun has not yet set on the flat sand, dimly seeing Lintao. Shen Bao Local Supplement Movie Special

Who is the Highest-Earning Star in Hollywood? (Part 1) 231

— Chen Xiong

A movie star, besides investing himself in the film industry to earn money for himself and support his personal life, must also consider the employer who hires him, to make money for the company. The result of this earning is that he can enjoy mutual benefits. Some movie stars only have their own reputation and generous salaries. After filming, the company spends huge production costs, but the result is that the film loses money, and the company suffers. Conversely, some movie stars, although not highly renowned and not paid handsomely, can make money from the dramas they act in, and the company is happy to hire them. Such stars are very rare and valuable.

Although there are many movie stars in Hollywood, not all of them can make money for the company. Many are hired by a company solely for the sake of the star's face. If we can find out which stars can make money, we can predict their future fortunes.

Perhaps what we are about to say will surprise the general reader, but we may as well state in advance that the following figures are based on the latest American film industry annual publication. They have compiled a detailed table for reference, listing all productions that have earned over one million US dollars since the beginning of American cinema. From this table, we can see who are the highest-earning stars in Hollywood, because stars who can earn over one million dollars for the company are generally the most popular among the audience. It can also be said that such stars can stand in the film industry forever.

Janet Gaynor is the highest-earning star in Hollywood. Among the films she starred in, seven productions earned over one million US dollars for the company. Five of them were with Charles Farrell as her partner. In terms of this achievement, the dramas that Janet Gaynor acted in catered to the psychology of the general audience more than any other Hollywood star. Although the comedic star Roscoe "Fatty" Arbuckle once insulted the Chinese in the film "The Cook," which was not pleasing to our countrymen, he is the second highest-earning star in Hollywood to earn over one million US dollars. Among the films he made, five productions exceeded one million in revenue. The third highest-earning person to earn over one million dollars is also a comedic performer, Charlie Chaplin. At the same time, the late romantic lead Rudolph Valentino and Fox's mainstay Warner Baxter can also be ranked third with Chaplin. Each of the above three people has three productions with more than one million in revenue. The remaining stars who have earned over one million US dollars for the company in two productions include Edmund Lowe, Richard Barthelmess, Wallace Beery, the late Ricardo Cortez, Ronald Colman, Bebe Daniels, Dolores del Río, Richard Dix, the late Marie Dressler, Greta Garbo, John Gilbert, Al Jolson, Dick Powell, Will Rogers, and Mae West. There are four stars – Mary Pickford, Douglas Fairbanks, Katharine Hepburn, and Constance Bennett – each with only one production that has earned over one million US dollars.

Although this table lists seventy-three films that have earned over one million US dollars, we will only cite a few familiar to our countrymen to illustrate the reasons why they made money. (To be continued)

Film Review

Review of "The Private Life of Don Juan" 232

— Ling He

Private Life of Don Juan 丨 Nanjing

Don Juan, this handsome hero of the Middle Ages, not only captivated many women in numerous romantic legends, but many young men also regarded him as the ideal typical warrior. Thus, Don Juan's fame had a great influence in society. Therefore, there was a silent film starring John Barrymore in "Don Juan," and now there is Fairbanks starring in "The Private Life of Don Juan," which is not without social basis.

Translated as "Beauty's Heart," "The Private Life of Don Juan," after "The Private Life of Henry VIII" and "The Rise of Catherine the Great," under the direction of Alexander Korda, is most successful in its merciless satire of this hero. Here, we are reminded of Cervantes' "Don Quixote," which mercilessly satirized the fallen knight. However, Pabst did not fully achieve this in the film. Don Quixote on the screen was given sympathy. But the Don Juan directed by Alexander Korda, unlike the "Don Juan" performed by John Barrymore, which praised and eulogized the great lover, aims to satirize Don Juan to the fullest.

Let us see how Don Juan's life is depicted here. In Spain, he is known as a great lover. He makes many young women betray their husbands and dedicate themselves to him. Just receiving a kiss from him is considered a great honor. Thus, under such great fame, there is the appearance of fake Don Juans by young rascals who fight to the death with the lover's husband. The real Don Juan's fame is thus extinguished. When a crowd of women mourns at the cemetery, our Don Juan is both amused and exasperated. It turns out that his honor is nothing more than a playful arrangement by people. Afterwards, he spends ten years of quiet time in a small inn under the guise of a fake general. Young women in their boudoirs recall his heroic appearance, and his biography is a best-seller, while the real Don Juan is constantly ridiculed or mocked. He is teased by old women, mocked by young maids, and treated like a father by another young woman. No one even plays with him anymore. Thus, he feels the loneliness of life. In years of bitter smiles, he shakes his spirit and hopes to transform the faces of the old into the brilliance of youth. But the dead young Don Juan is no longer understood by people. When he returns to Seville, the singer who once loved him passionately does not recognize him. He is embarrassingly mocked by women in the theater. Although his wife finally receives him, he deeply experiences the bitterness of life. What is revealed to us from these scenes is a bitter and laughing life. This Don Juan, from glory to decline, gives people some degree of sympathy, but this sympathy is emitted in cruel ridicule.

Furthermore, under the director's technique, Don Juan is a comical character. When he has intimate meetings with women, every time it is the same few words of praise, which is no different from the fake Don Juan falling down the stairs. Especially the various things after he returns to Seville in his old age, to the point of climbing the stairs to have an intimate meeting with his wife, all show his pitiful comedy. After we have seen this film, the taste of life's bitterness heavily assaults our hearts.

In terms of performance, perhaps the director and screenwriter are slightly disorganized in the first part. But on the whole, it is still very successful. To illustrate this point, we can cite the charming dance of the dancer André, as well as the scene of many groups of black-clad women in mourning, the jealousy of the real and fake lovers, and Don Juan's expressions of being unable to cry or laugh, all of which can prove Alexander Korda's refined technique.

Moreover, due to the excellent photography and the combination of sound effects and scenes, we deeply realize the scenery of medieval Spain from the beautiful night streets, from the passionate songs of the ukulele, and from the daring women. Especially due to Merle Oberon's excellent acting, the dance coming down from the building is truly too captivating. As for Fairbanks' acting, it is quite insufficient. His rude movements are not enough to express the so-called great lover's dashing and affectionate nature. He is just a demon who teases women.

Fairbanks' Comeback: Enchanting Butterfly and Blooming Spring in "The Private Life of Don Juan" 233

— Heng Yun

London Films in England produced the amazing "The Private Life of Henry VIII" in 1933 and discovered Charles Laughton's talent. In 1934, they produced "The Rise of Catherine the Great" and established Bergner's position in the art world. At the same time, Elstree in England resembled Hollywood in the United States, building a solid barrier. Whose achievement is this? I am afraid that if Elstree in England did not have Alexander Korda's directorial genius, the films of the Old World would not have attracted the world's attention until now. This is an undeniable fact.

The first and first-class martial arts romantic superstar since the beginning of silver history, the well-known Fairbanks, his success lies in fully performing the spirit of Bushido. Of course, the modern style is definitely not suitable for his unique personality. Therefore, masterpieces such as "The Three Musketeers," "The Thief of Bagdad," and "The Black Pirate" can only be tried by him. He could have lived leisurely in the forest, without having to wear a crown and long sword, agile and energetic on the screen. (According to the official divorce from Mary Pickford this time, it is the prelude to Fairbanks' marriage to a certain noblewoman in London. After that, Fairbanks may be knighted and enter the ranks of the nobility. Therefore, in the film "The Private Life of Don Juan," he is titled as Mr. Fairbanks.) But Fairbanks finally accepted Korda as the director (all of Fairbanks' films were directed by himself) and made "The Private Life of Don Juan," the secret history of the great lover of the 19th century.

Since "The Private Life of Don Juan" belongs to British filmmakers, it is regarded as the greatest film of 1935, so even the supporting roles have been carefully managed. They claim that the beauties in "The Private Life of Don Juan" are selected from the four corners of the island country. The heroine, Merle Oberon, is in her youth, and is the result of Fairbanks' several strict selections, while Binnie Barnes, Benita Hume, Penelope Dudley-Ward, and Joan Gardner are all famous stars in the film industry. As for the recording, location shooting, and processing intentions, they are all top-notch. Indeed, this is a major threat that Elstree in England has given to Hollywood in 1935.

A Collection of Art-China Film Studio Anecdotes 234

In Shi Dongshan's directed sound film "Human Affairs," the role of the female lead was originally set to be played by Wang Ying. After filming several scenes, there was a sudden objection, saying that the personality was not expressed, and she was unwilling to play the role of an old woman. Shi Dongshan believed that Wang was unwilling to play this role, so he could not force it, so it has been changed to be played by Hu Ping.

Hu Tong's directed musical singing film "Elegy of Life" and Dan Duyu's directed sound dialogue song Tang film "The Night Before the Wedding" are both scheduled to be released around the end of the lunar year.

Yuan Congmei's written and directed "The Storm" (that is, the name of "The Sacrifice" has been changed) will begin filming.

Yue Feng directed, Kang Na assisted, Yuan Meiyun, Wang Yin, Yuan Congmei, Ye Juanjuan, Cang Yinqiu and others co-starred in the musical singing film "The Escape," and the result is imminent.

Bu Wancang's written and directed "Triumphal Song" will also begin filming.

Yan Youxiang and Zheng Yingshi went to southern China to inspect the business conditions of various theaters. Now Yan has completed his official business and returned to Shanghai, and Zheng is also about to return.

"The Night Before the Wedding" has achieved excellent results, and the sound, photography, performance, and directorial techniques have special achievements.

Film Novel

The Legend of the Red Sheep Hero (4) 235

— Zhao Chu

The crowd gave Xiao a way back. Instead, he grabbed the troublemaker, lifted him high and threw him away. The troublemaker was thrown into the muddy river and struggled endlessly. Seeing that the situation was not good, and after being driven away by Qin and Xiao, the crowd dispersed. Hong Feng immediately stepped forward to thank Qin and Xiao. After Hong Feng and Qin Xiao met, Yang Xiuqing also stepped forward. Hong clasped his hands and thanked them: "Thank you both for your great help, otherwise we would have been besieged." Qin replied: "I saw that they were too arrogant and unreasonable, and I was afraid that you would suffer, so I came out to help." Xiao also replied: "I am always ready to fight for justice, what is this?" Hong Feng was very humble and greeted them, saying: "It is rare for us to meet today, please sit in the hotel in front for a while."

Wine cups and dishes were placed on the table, and half of them had already been eaten. Hong Feng, Qin Xiao, and Yang sat together. Hong raised the filled wine and persuaded everyone to drink a cup. Then Hong put down the wine cup and continued to say: "So although I have experienced these setbacks, I do not retreat. Now the most important thing is to wake up the compatriots who are sleeping in dreams." Qin Rigang, after hearing these words, said with joy: "Mr. Hong's words penetrate into my heart. I am willing to follow you for life as an ordinary soldier." He immediately stood up, walked to Hong's side, bowed and knelt down. Hong repeatedly stood up and asked him to sit down. Xiao Chaogui also cupped his hands and said: "I, Xiao Chaogui, have a lot of strength, but nowhere to use it. If Mr. Hong looks up to me and can use me, there will be a place to spill my blood." Hong Feng repeatedly thanked them, saying: "Thank you for your kindness, but I hate that I am incompetent and unworthy, and I dare not accept it." He then raised his cup and persuaded everyone to drink another cup. Yang Xiuqing put down his cup, pondered for a while, and said to Hong Feng: "You two should have a base of operations now, so it will be easy to develop." Hong sighed and said: "This is exactly our difficulty. We are being watched by officials in Guangdong, and we are unfamiliar with the place in Guangxi." Yang Xiuqing then smiled and said: "I can recommend a place, which is at the home of Zeng Yuxuan in Jintian Village. He is a big landlord here, and he is also ambitious. He is unwilling to be an official and likes to make friends. If Mr. Hong is willing to go, I think he will be very welcome." Hong Feng listened, and both showed joy, saying: "This is the best. How can we not be willing to go?" Yang then nodded and said: "The opportunity is really a coincidence. This time we are escorting loan silver to his village. It is just right to go together." Hong was extremely excited when he heard this, and tied up his luggage, saying: "This is really a heaven-sent opportunity. Perhaps our career will be created here!" Saying this, Xiao Chaogui grabbed the wine pot and poured wine in front of everyone, and they all raised their glasses to congratulate them.

Hong Xiuquan settled in Jintian Village, and Zeng Yuxuan hit it off. Yang and Xiao also closed their security bureau and gathered in Jintian Village. Soon, they founded the Baoliang Bandit Suppression Association to plot major events together. On the side of the door of the Baoliang Bandit Suppression Association, a note was posted saying that the Baoliang Bandit Suppression Association was recruiting. Two tables were set up by the door, with many registration books placed on them. Many people came to apply and were registered one by one. Yang Xiuqing was monitoring, and Xiao Chaogui and Qin Rigang were checking the physique of the people who came, while chanting their names.

One day, Zeng Yuxuan, Hong Xiuquan, and Yang Xiuqing were sitting there discussing major events. Suddenly, a servant walked in and said: "A person has come outside and wants to see the master and Mr. Hong. When asked for his name, he refused to say." The three hesitated for a moment and said: "Go and invite him in." Yang Xiuqing immediately put away the registration books. Suddenly, a big man walked in at the door, with a very serious expression on his face, and said loudly: "You are using the name of the Baoliang Association here to recruit soldiers and buy horses, plotting against the imperial court. Aren't you afraid of being killed? You can deceive others, but you can't deceive me!" When he said this, his expression was very stern. The three of them were stunned by him. Zeng Yuxuan turned around to take the sword hanging on the wall. The man laughed loudly when he saw it and said: "You have good eyesight, but you don't recognize me, Shi Dakai?" Zeng put down his sword, and the three understood. Hong Xiuquan changed his face and smiled: "Are you Mr. Shi Dakai?" (To be continued)
